name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

    def importtestmodule(
        path: Path,
        config: Config,
    ):
        # We assume we are only called once per module.
        importmode = config.getoption("--import-mode")
        try:
            mod = import_path(
                path,
                mode=importmode,
                root=config.rootpath,
                consider_namespace_packages=config.getini("consider_namespace_packages"),
            )
        except SyntaxError as e:
            raise nodes.Collector.CollectError(
                ExceptionInfo.from_current().getrepr(style="short")
            ) from e
        except ImportPathMismatchError as e:
            raise nodes.Collector.CollectError(
                "import file mismatch:\n"
                "imported module {!r} has this __file__ attribute:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "which is not the same as the test file we want to collect:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "HINT: remove __pycache__ / .pyc files and/or use a "
                "unique basename for your test file modules".format(*e.args)
            ) from e
        except ImportError as e:
            exc_info = ExceptionInfo.from_current()
            if config.get_verbosity() < 2:
                exc_info.traceback = exc_info.traceback.filter(filter_traceback)
            exc_repr = (
                exc_info.getrepr(style="short")

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

    def importtestmodule(
        path: Path,
        config: Config,
    ):
        # We assume we are only called once per module.
        importmode = config.getoption("--import-mode")
        try:
            mod = import_path(
                path,
                mode=importmode,
                root=config.rootpath,
                consider_namespace_packages=config.getini("consider_namespace_packages"),
            )
        except SyntaxError as e:

                ExceptionInfo.from_current().getrepr(style="short")
            ) from e

                "imported module {!r} has this __file__ attribute:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "which is not the same as the test file we want to collect:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "HINT: remove __pycache__ / .pyc files and/or use a "
                "unique basename for your test file modules".format(*e.args)
            ) from e

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "

            for character in name:
                if character != '.':

    def importtestmodule(
        path: Path,
        config: Config,
    ):
        # We assume we are only called once per module.
        importmode = config.getoption("--import-mode")
        try:
            mod = import_path(
                path,
                mode=importmode,
                root=config.rootpath,
                consider_namespace_packages=config.getini("consider_namespace_packages"),
            )
        except SyntaxError as e:

                ExceptionInfo.from_current().getrepr(style="short")
            ) from e
        except ImportPathMismatchError as e:
            raise nodes.Collector.CollectError(
                "import file mismatch:\n"
                "imported module {!r} has this __file__ attribute:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "which is not the same as the test file we want to collect:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "HINT: remove __pycache__ / .pyc files and/or use a "
                "unique basename for your test file modules".format(*e.args)
            ) from e
        except ImportError as e:
            exc_info = ExceptionInfo.from_current()
            if config.get_verbosity() < 2:

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.

    def importtestmodule(

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1

    def importtestmodule(
        path: Path,
        config: Config,
    ):
        # We assume we are only called once per module.
        importmode = config.getoption("--import-mode")
        try:
            mod = import_path(
                path,
                mode=importmode,
                root=config.rootpath,
                consider_namespace_packages=config.getini("consider_namespace_packages"),

                "  {}\n"
                "which is not the same as the test file we want to collect:\n"
                "  {}\n"
                "HINT: remove __pycache__ / .pyc files and/or use a "
                "unique basename for your test file modules".format(*e.args)
            ) from e

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1

    def importtestmodule(

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the

    def importtestmodule(

                "  {}\n"

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
>       return _bootstrap._gcd_import(name[level:], package, level)

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':

name = 'vendor.pyedflib', package = None

    def import_module(name, package=None):
        """Import a module.
    
        The 'package' argument is required when performing a relative import. It
        specifies the package to use as the anchor point from which to resolve the
        relative import to an absolute import.
    
        """
        level = 0
        if name.startswith('.'):
            if not package:
                raise TypeError("the 'package' argument is required to perform a "
                                f"relative import for {name!r}")
            for character in name:
                if character != '.':
                    break
                level += 1
